<meta name="description" content="周瑜（175年-210年），字公瑾，庐江（今安徽庐江县西南）人 。东汉末年名将，洛阳令周异之子，堂祖父周景、堂叔周忠，都官至太尉。长壮有姿貌、精音律，江东有“曲有误，周郎顾”之语。周瑜少与孙策交好，21岁起随孙策奔赴战场平定江东，后孙策遇刺身亡，孙权继任，周瑜将兵赴丧，以中护军的身份与长史张昭共掌众事。建安十三年 （208年），周瑜率军与刘备联合，于赤壁之战中大败曹操，由此奠定了“三分天下”的基础。又率军大破曹仁，拜偏将军领南郡太守。建安十五年（210年）病逝于巴丘，年仅36岁。正史上周瑜“性度恢廓”“实奇才也”，孙权称赞周瑜有“王佐之资&quot;，范成大誉之为“世间豪杰英雄士、江左风流美丈夫”。宋徽宗时追尊其为平虏伯。位列唐武庙六十四将、宋武庙七十二将之一。...">

<dd class="lemmaWgt-lemmaTitle-title">
<span class="lemma-pinyin" >
<span class="text">[zhōu yú]</span>
<a class="speak" id="j-pinyin-speak" href="javascript:;" title="点击发声" nslog-type="10000106">&nbsp;</a>
</span>
<div id="fmp_flash_div" style="position:absolute; left:-9999px;">

<h1 >周瑜</h1>
<h2>（汉末时期东吴名将）</h2>
<a href="javascript:;" class="edit-lemma cmn-btn-hover-blue cmn-btn-28 j-edit-link"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_edit-lemma"></em>编辑</a>
<a class="lock-lemma" nslog-type="10003105" target="_blank" href="javascript:;" title="锁定"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_lock-lemma"></em>锁定</a>
<a href="/planet/talk?lemmaId=17342" target="_blank" class="lemma-discussion cmn-btn-hover-blue cmn-btn-28 j-discussion-link" nslog-type="90000102"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_discussion-solid"></em>讨论<span class="num">999</span></a>
</dd>
</dl><div class="promotion-declaration">
</div><div class="lemma-summary" label-module="lemmaSummary">
<div class="para" label-module="para">周瑜（175年-210年），字公瑾，庐江（今<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AE%89%E5%BE%BD">安徽</a>庐江县西南<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="1-2" data-ctrmap=":1,:2,">
[1-2]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[1-2]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
）人 。东汉末年名将，洛阳令<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E5%BC%82/3081661" data-lemmaid="3081661">周异</a>之子，堂祖父<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E6%99%AF/3294035" data-lemmaid="3294035">周景</a>、堂叔<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E5%BF%A0/17833916" data-lemmaid="17833916">周忠</a>，都官至<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%A4%AA%E5%B0%89/32091" data-lemmaid="32091">太尉</a>。长壮有姿貌、精音律，<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%B1%9F%E4%B8%9C">江东</a>有“曲有误，周郎顾”之语。</div><div class="para" label-module="para">周瑜少与<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E7%AD%96">孙策</a>交好，21岁起随孙策奔赴战场平定江东，后孙策遇刺身亡，<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E6%9D%83">孙权</a>继任，周瑜将兵赴丧，以中护军的身份与长史<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%BC%A0%E6%98%AD">张昭</a>共掌众事。建安十三年 （208年），周瑜率军与<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%88%98%E5%A4%87">刘备</a>联合，于<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%B5%A4%E5%A3%81%E4%B9%8B%E6%88%98">赤壁之战</a>中大败<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9B%B9%E6%93%8D/6772" data-lemmaid="6772">曹操</a>，由此奠定了“三分天下”的基础。又率军大破<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9B%B9%E4%BB%81/6767" data-lemmaid="6767">曹仁</a>，拜偏将军领南郡太守。建安十五年（210年）病逝于巴丘，年仅36岁。</div><div class="para" label-module="para">正史上周瑜“性度恢廓”“实奇才也”，孙权称赞周瑜有“王佐之资&quot;，<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%8C%83%E6%88%90%E5%A4%A7">范成大</a>誉之为“世间豪杰英雄士、江左风流美丈夫”。宋徽宗时追尊其为平虏伯。位列唐武庙六十四将、宋武庙七十二将之一。</div>
</div>

<div class="hotspotminingContent_pic ">
<a href="https://baike.baidu.com/tashuo/browse/content?id=4507e4544fa413e14c612d60&lemmaId=17342&lemmaId=17342&fr=qingtian" target="_blank"><img src="https://gss1.bdstatic.com/9vo3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/whfpf%3D180%2C140%2C50/sign=e55c7b8098eef01f4d414b8586c3a81d/242dd42a2834349b52e8ac61c5ea15ce37d3be6c.jpg" /></a>

<div class="hotspotminingContent_cnt ">
<div class="hotspotminingContent_cnt_tit"><span class="hotspotminingContent_cnt_tit_tit"><a href="https://baike.baidu.com/tashuo/browse/content?id=4507e4544fa413e14c612d60&lemmaId=17342&lemmaId=17342&fr=qingtian" target="_blank">若非此人英年早逝，三国时期是否真会实现二分天下</a></span><img src="https://bkssl.bdimg.com/static/wiki-lemma/widget/lemma_content/configModule/hotspotmining/img/flag_new_c80aa2a.png" />
<span class="hotspotminingContent_cnt_tit_tim">2018-07-10 21:07</span>
</div>
<div class="hotspotminingContent_cnt_cnt">
<span>江东不是中原，江东政权是比较平稳打下的，惨烈战斗不多，多是对世家大族的妥协，世家大族实力在东吴根深蒂固。
东吴将领均有属于家族和个人的私兵，其必须维护家族利益。在危机关头，为维护自家利益，凭借长江天险，以己所长水战防御尚可，但要为孙权与刘备集团死磕，恐怕没多少人愿意。况且陆战吴军并不擅长。</span><a href="https://baike.baidu.com/tashuo/browse/content?id=4507e4544fa413e14c612d60&lemmaId=17342&lemmaId=17342&fr=qingtian" target="_blank">...详情</a></div>

<a name="1" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_1" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="人物生平" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-2" label-module="para-title">
<h2 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>人物生平</h2>
<a class="edit-icon j-edit-link" data-edit-dl="1" href="javascript:;"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_edit-lemma"></em>编辑</a>
</div>
<div class="anchor-list">
<a name="1_1" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_1_1" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="官宦世家" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="1-1" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>官宦世家</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">周瑜出身大族，他的堂祖父<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E6%99%AF/3294035" data-lemmaid="3294035">周景</a>、堂叔<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E5%BF%A0/17833916" data-lemmaid="17833916">周忠</a>，都官居汉朝<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%A4%AA%E5%B0%89">太尉</a>之职。其父<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E5%BC%82">周异</a>，曾任洛阳令。周瑜本人身材高大、相貌俊美，志向远大。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">初平元年（190年），孙坚兵讨<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%91%A3%E5%8D%93">董卓</a>时，他家人住在寿春，当时孙坚长子孙策与周瑜同年出生，而且在江淮一带很有名气。周瑜慕名前去拜访，劝孙策带母亲弟弟移居庐江舒县，<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E7%AD%96/17360" data-lemmaid="17360">孙策</a>听从了他的意见<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="3" data-ctrmap=":3,">
[3]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[3]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
。周瑜让出路南的大宅院供孙家居住，且登堂拜见孙策的母亲，两家交好。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="4" data-ctrmap=":4,">
[4]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[4]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
初平二年（191年），孙坚死后，<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E7%AD%96">孙策</a>带家人搬离了庐江<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="3" data-ctrmap=":3,">
[3]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[3]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="1_2" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_1_2" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="丹阳借兵" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="1-2" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>丹阳借兵</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><sub>主词条：<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E7%AD%96%E5%B9%B3%E6%B1%9F%E4%B8%9C%E4%B9%8B%E6%88%98">孙策平江东之战</a></sub></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">兴平二年（195年）周瑜前去探望身为丹阳太守的从父周尚。正好孙策率军入<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%8E%86%E9%98%B3">历阳</a>（今安徽和县西<a class="lemma-album layout-right nslog:10000206" title="周瑜"  href="/pic/%E5%91%A8%E7%91%9C/17342/23780219/0db2c9ca3d50ed0df31fe74c?fr=lemma&ct=cover" target="_blank"  style="width:140px;" nslog-type="10000206">
<div class="album-wrap" style="width:138px;height:220px;">
<img class="picture" alt="周瑜" src="https://gss2.bdstatic.com/-fo3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=f5820c8fb74543a9f11bfdce2e168a7b/8b13632762d0f703d71447a708fa513d2697c523.jpg" style="width:138px;height:220px;"/>
</div>
<div class="description">
周瑜<span class="number">(6张)</span>
</div>
<div class="albumBg">
<div class="albumBgFir" style="width:132px;"></div>
<div class="albumBgSec" style="width:126px;"></div>
</div>
</a>
北），将要东渡长江，于是写信给周瑜。周瑜率兵迎接孙策，给他以大力支持。孙策十分喜悦，说：“我有了你，事就成了。”<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="5" data-ctrmap=":5,">
[5]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[5]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">于是，周瑜随从孙策先克<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%A8%AA%E6%B1%9F/10181504" data-lemmaid="10181504">横江</a>（今安徽和县东南长江北岸）、当利（今安徽和县东，当利水入江处），接着挥师渡江，进攻<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%A7%A3%E9%99%B5">秣陵</a>（今南京江宁秣陵关），打败了<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%AC%AE%E8%9E%8D">笮融</a>、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%96%9B%E7%A4%BC/2205333" data-lemmaid="2205333">薛礼</a>，转而攻占湖孰（今南京江宁湖熟镇）、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%B1%9F%E4%B9%98">江乘</a>，进入<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9B%B2%E9%98%BF">曲阿</a>（今江苏丹阳），逼走<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%88%98%E7%B9%87">刘繇</a>。当时孙策部众已发展到几万人。他对周瑜说：“我用这支队伍攻取吴郡、会稽郡，平定山越，已经足够了，你回去镇守丹阳。”于是，周瑜率部回到丹阳。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="6" data-ctrmap=":6,">
[6]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[6]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">不久，<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%A2%81%E6%9C%AF/16976" data-lemmaid="16976">袁术</a>派其堂弟<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%A2%81%E8%83%A4">袁胤</a>取代<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E5%B0%9A/12281344" data-lemmaid="12281344">周尚</a>任丹阳太守，周瑜随周尚到了<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AF%BF%E6%98%A5">寿春</a>（今安徽寿县）。袁术发现周瑜有才，便欲收罗周瑜为已将。周瑜看出袁术最终不会有什么成就，所以只请求做居巢县长，欲借机回江东，袁术同意了周瑜的请求。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="7-8" data-ctrmap=":7,:8,">
[7-8]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[7-8]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">周瑜在做<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%B1%85%E5%B7%A2%E5%8E%BF">居巢县</a>长认识了<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%B2%81%E8%82%83/9396" data-lemmaid="9396">鲁肃</a>，认为他非同寻常，就主动与他相交，两人建立了如同春秋时<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%85%AC%E5%AD%99%E4%BE%A8">公孙侨</a>和<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AD%A3%E6%9C%AD">季札</a>那样牢不可破的朋友关系<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="9" data-ctrmap=":9,">
[9]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[9]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="1_3" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_1_3" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="官居要职" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="1-3" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>官居要职</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:118px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" nslog-type="9317"
			href="/pic/%E5%91%A8%E7%91%9C/17342/0/eaf81a4c510fd9f9dc2a564a282dd42a2834a4d7?fr=lemma&ct=single" target="_blank"
		title="周郎顾曲" style="width:118px;height:220px;">
<img  class="lazy-img" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" data-src="https://gss3.bdstatic.com/-Po3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=b3999f1241086e066ea8384932087b5a/eaf81a4c510fd9f9dc2a564a282dd42a2834a4d7.jpg"  alt="周郎顾曲" style="width:118px;height:220px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
周郎顾曲
<sup>[10]</sup>
<a name="ref_[10]_"></a>
</span>
</div>建安三年（198年），周瑜和鲁肃一同回到<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%90%B4%E9%83%A1">吴郡</a>（今江苏苏州）。孙策闻周瑜归来，亲自出迎，授周瑜<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%BB%BA%E5%A8%81%E4%B8%AD%E9%83%8E%E5%B0%86">建威中郎将</a>，调拨给他士兵两千人，战骑五十匹。此外，孙策还赐给周瑜鼓吹乐队，替周瑜修建住所，赏赐之厚，无人能与之相比。<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E7%AD%96">孙策</a>还在发布的命令中说：“周公瑾雄姿英发，才能绝伦，和我有<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%80%BB%E8%A7%92">总角</a>之好，骨肉之情。在丹阳时，他率领兵众，调发船粮相助于我，使我能成就大事，论功酬德，赏赐还远不能回报他在关键时刻给我的支持呢！”周瑜时年二十四岁，吴郡人皆称之为周郎。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="11" data-ctrmap=":11,">
[11]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[11]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">因庐江一带，士民向来佩服周瑜的恩德信义，于是孙策命他出守<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%89%9B%E6%B8%9A">牛渚</a>、后来又兼任春谷长。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">建安四年（199年）孙策要攻打荆州，拜周瑜为<a target=_blank href="/item/%E4%B8%AD%E6%8A%A4%E5%86%9B">中护军</a>，兼任<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%B1%9F%E5%A4%8F/889390" data-lemmaid="889390">江夏</a>（治湖北新州西）太守，随军征讨。十二月，孙策率周瑜等人攻破<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%9A%96%E5%9F%8E">皖城</a>，虏获袁术手下<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%88%98%E5%8B%8B/8444731" data-lemmaid="8444731">刘勋</a>家人及他们部下的男女亲族，其中桥公二女皆国色天姿，孙策自纳<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%A4%A7%E4%B9%94">大乔</a>，周瑜纳<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%B0%8F%E4%B9%94">小乔</a>。孙策对周瑜说：“桥公之女，虽经战乱流离之苦，但得我们二人作女婿，也足可庆幸了。”接着进攻寻阳，败<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%88%98%E5%8B%8B/8444731" data-lemmaid="8444731">刘勋</a>，第二年年初讨江夏，又回兵平定豫章（今江西南昌）、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%BA%90%E9%99%B5">庐陵</a>（今江西吉安）。周瑜留下来镇守<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%B7%B4%E4%B8%98">巴丘</a>。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="7" data-ctrmap=":7,:12,">
[7]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[7]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="12" data-ctrmap=":7,:12,">
[12]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[12]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="1_4" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_1_4" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="安邦重臣" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="1-4" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>安邦重臣</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">建安五年（200年）四月，孙策遇刺身亡，时年26岁，临终把军国大事托付<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E6%9D%83">孙权</a>。孙权统业时，年龄尚小，只有<a target=_blank href="/item/%E4%BC%9A%E7%A8%BD">会稽</a>、吴郡、丹阳、豫章、庐陵数郡，其偏远险要之处也尚未全附。天下英雄豪杰散在各个州郡，并未和孙氏建立起君臣之间相互依赖的关系。张昭和周瑜等人认为孙权能与他们一起成就大业，所以倾心服侍他<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="13" data-ctrmap=":13,">
[13]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[13]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">周瑜从外地带兵前来奔丧，留在吴郡孙权身边任中护军，同<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%95%BF%E5%8F%B2">长史</a><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%BC%A0%E6%98%AD/4330" data-lemmaid="4330">张昭</a>共同掌管军政大事。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="14" data-ctrmap=":14,">
[14]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[14]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
当时孙权只是将军，宾客礼节都很简单，唯独周瑜用君臣的礼节表达对孙权的支持<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="15" data-ctrmap=":15,">
[15]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[15]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">周瑜一次对鲁肃说道：“过去<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%A9%AC%E6%8F%B4/3606" data-lemmaid="3606">马援</a>答复光武帝说过，‘当今之世，非但君择臣，臣亦择君’。如今我的主人孙权亲信贤人智士，接纳奇才异能，我听说古代哲人的神秘论证，接承天命替代刘氏者，必定起于东南，推算历数观察形势，最终会造建起帝王基业，与天命相符合，也正在东南。正是有识有志之士归附英杰的时代。我正通晓此理啊！”<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="16" data-ctrmap=":16,">
[16]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[16]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
<a name="ref_16"></a>并向孙权推荐鲁肃，说他有才干，可为辅佐之臣。建议孙权应该多方搜罗鲁肃这样的人才，以成就大业，不能让他们流散外地。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="16" data-ctrmap=":16,">
[16]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[16]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
<a name="ref_16"></a></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">曹操在<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AE%98%E6%B8%A1%E4%B9%8B%E6%88%98">官渡之战</a>打败<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%A2%81%E7%BB%8D">袁绍</a>后，在建安七年（202年），下书责令孙权送人质到曹操这里。孙权便召集群臣会商。大臣们众说纷纭，张昭、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%A7%A6%E6%9D%BE/857407" data-lemmaid="857407">秦松</a>等重臣犹豫再三，不能决断。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">孙权本意不想送人质。于是，他只带周瑜一人到母亲面前议定此事。周瑜分析道：“当年楚君刚被封到荆山的<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:138px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" nslog-type="9317"
			href="/pic/%E5%91%A8%E7%91%9C/17342/0/8694a4c27d1ed21b2a01b90ca06eddc450da3f0a?fr=lemma&ct=single" target="_blank"
		title="周瑜雕像" style="width:138px;height:220px;">
<img  class="lazy-img" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" data-src="https://gss0.bdstatic.com/-4o3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=2dd67f8d5b4e9258a23481ecac80d1d1/8694a4c27d1ed21b2a01b90ca06eddc450da3f0a.jpg"  alt="周瑜雕像" style="width:138px;height:220px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
周瑜雕像
</span>
</div>边上时，地方不够百里。他的后辈贤能，扩张土地，开拓疆域，在<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%83%A2%E9%83%BD">郢都</a>建立根基，占据荆扬之地，直到南海。子孙代代相传，延续九百多年。将军您继承父兄的余威旧业，统御六郡，兵精粮足，战士们士气旺盛。而且，铸山为铜，煮海为盐，人心安定，士风强劲，可以说<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%89%80%E5%90%91%E6%97%A0%E6%95%8C">所向无敌</a>，为什么要送质于人呢？人质一到曹操手下，我们就不得不与曹操相呼应，也就必然受制于曹氏。那时，我们所能得到的最大的利益，也不过就是一方侯印、十几个仆人、几辆车、几匹马罢了，哪能跟我们自己创建功业，称孤道寡相提并论呢？为今之计，最好是不送人质，先静观曹操的动向和变化。如果曹操能遵守道义，拯救天下，那时我们再归附也不晚；如果曹操骄纵，图谋生乱玩火必自焚，将军您只要静待天命即可，为何要送质于人呢？”周瑜这番话，说到了孙权心里。孙权的母亲也认为该这样做，她对孙权说：“公瑾的话有道理，他比你哥哥只小1个月，我一向把他当儿子对待，你该把他当成兄长才是。”孙权便没给曹操送人质。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="17" data-ctrmap=":17,">
[17]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[17]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E6%9D%83">孙权</a>每次下赐周瑜，一年到头都有一百件衣服，当时没有那个将领能与周瑜相比<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="18" data-ctrmap=":18,">
[18]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[18]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
。对于孙氏，周瑜也说得上忠贞不二。《<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%B1%9F%E8%A1%A8%E4%BC%A0">江表传</a>》记载，曹操想使周瑜为自己所用，曾派善于辩说的<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%92%8B%E5%B9%B2">蒋干</a>前去游说周瑜， 周瑜既十分坚决的回绝了蒋干。天下的<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%A3%AB%E4%BA%BA">士人</a>，因此愈加佩服周瑜。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">建安十一年（206年），周瑜率<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E7%91%9C/6279" data-lemmaid="6279">孙瑜</a>等讨伐麻、保二屯，斩其首领，俘万余人。江夏太守<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%BB%84%E7%A5%96">黄祖</a>遣部将<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%82%93%E9%BE%99/4197656" data-lemmaid="4197656">邓龙</a>率数千人进攻<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9F%B4%E6%A1%91">柴桑</a>，周瑜率军反击，俘虏了邓龙。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="19" data-ctrmap=":19,">
[19]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[19]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
黄祖的将领<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%94%98%E5%AE%81/7048" data-lemmaid="7048">甘宁</a>前来归降，周瑜和吕蒙一起推荐他，因此受到了孙权的重用<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="20" data-ctrmap=":20,">
[20]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[20]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">建安十三年（208年）春，孙权征讨江夏的<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%BB%84%E7%A5%96/17037" data-lemmaid="17037">黄祖</a>。周瑜为前部大督，抓获黄祖。孙权下令斩首黄祖。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="21" data-ctrmap=":21,">
[21]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[21]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="1_5" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_1_5" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="联刘破曹" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="1-5" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>联刘破曹</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><sub>主词条：<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%B5%A4%E5%A3%81%E4%B9%8B%E6%88%98/81515" data-lemmaid="81515">赤壁之战</a></sub></div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">建安十三年（208年）秋天，<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9B%B9%E6%93%8D/6772" data-lemmaid="6772">曹操</a>率军南侵，占领荆州，曹操向孙权进逼。大军压境之际，孙权本意与曹操一战，向下询问计策。然而孙权的大臣们出现了主和、主战两派<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:220px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" nslog-type="9317"
			href="/pic/%E5%91%A8%E7%91%9C/17342/0/54fbb2fb43166d227f3bde4f4c2309f79152d299?fr=lemma&ct=single" target="_blank"
		title="赤壁之战地图" style="width:220px;height:191px;">
<img  class="lazy-img" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" data-src="https://gss0.bdstatic.com/94o3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=43fc579c3312b31bc36cca2bb6193674/54fbb2fb43166d227f3bde4f4c2309f79152d299.jpg"  alt="赤壁之战地图" style="width:220px;height:191px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
赤壁之战地图
</span>
</div>，重臣谋士张昭和秦松更是支持投降曹操。于是鲁肃劝孙权招回在<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%84%B1%E9%98%B3">鄱阳</a>的周瑜。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">周瑜回到孙权身边，向孙权分析曹操与孙权两军的胜败关键，先是指出：曹军远途跋涉，疲惫不堪；天气寒冷，马没有草吃；北方人惯习陆战不擅水战，水土不服；马超、韩遂尚在关西，为曹操的后患。既而进一步分析了曹军的实际力量，指出来自中原的曹军不过十五六万，而且所得<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%88%98%E8%A1%A8/35154" data-lemmaid="35154">刘表</a>新降的七八万人，人心并不向曹。孙权感叹道：“曹操想要废汉自立很久了，只是忌讳二袁、吕布、刘表和我罢了。只留下我，我和曹操势不两立，你所说的话甚合我意，这是天把你赐给我了！”</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">孙权最终下定决心，拔剑砍掉桌子一角，说：“再有敢说投降的人，就像这个桌子一样！”<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="22" data-ctrmap=":22,">
[22]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[22]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">孙权命周瑜及<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%A8%8B%E6%99%AE/69841" data-lemmaid="69841">程普</a>等领三万人抗曹，途中在<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%B5%A4%E5%A3%81/9108057" data-lemmaid="9108057">赤壁</a>两军遇上，曹操军因有疾病，又不习水性，初战便败退，曹操引军至江北。周瑜便与刘备军在南岸设营<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="23" data-ctrmap=":23,">
[23]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[23]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
，双方<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AF%B9%E5%B3%99/3524" data-lemmaid="3524">对峙</a>。周瑜部将<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%BB%84%E7%9B%96/17341" data-lemmaid="17341">黄盖</a>建议用火计将曹军打败<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="24" data-ctrmap=":24,">
[24]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[24]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
，周瑜认为可行，命黄盖诈降<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="25" data-ctrmap=":25,">
[25]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[25]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
。曹操果然中计，船舰全被烧毁，曹操北还南郡。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="26" data-ctrmap=":26,">
[26]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[26]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="1_6" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_1_6" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="大破曹仁" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="1-6" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>大破曹仁</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">周瑜又与<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%A8%8B%E6%99%AE/69841" data-lemmaid="69841">程普</a>进军<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%8D%97%E9%83%A1">南郡</a>，和<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9B%B9%E4%BB%81/6767" data-lemmaid="6767">曹仁</a>隔江相持。两军尚未交锋，周瑜先派<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%94%98%E5%AE%81/7048" data-lemmaid="7048">甘宁</a>前去占据<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%A4%B7%E9%99%B5">夷陵</a>。曹仁分出一部分兵<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:220px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" nslog-type="9317"
			href="/pic/%E5%91%A8%E7%91%9C/17342/0/f7246b600c3387447121b9955c0fd9f9d62aa077?fr=lemma&ct=single" target="_blank"
		title="周瑜雕像" style="width:220px;height:165px;">
<img  class="lazy-img" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" data-src="https://gss2.bdstatic.com/9fo3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=9dd18be11230e924cba49b337c0a6e66/f7246b600c3387447121b9955c0fd9f9d62aa077.jpg"  alt="周瑜雕像" style="width:220px;height:165px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
周瑜雕像
</span>
</div>马包围了甘宁，甘宁向周瑜告急。周瑜采用了<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%90%95%E8%92%99/6432" data-lemmaid="6432">吕蒙</a>的计谋，留下<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%87%8C%E7%BB%9F/8708" data-lemmaid="8708">凌统</a>守卫后方，率军驰援夷陵，大破曹军于夷陵城下，所杀过半。曹军乘夜逃走，途经木柴堵塞的险路，无奈，骑马者皆弃马徒行。周瑜率兵追赶截击，获得战马三百匹，军威大振。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">周瑜率兵屯驻北岸，约定日期大战曹仁。周瑜亲自骑马督战，被飞箭射中右胁，伤势严重，退兵回营。曹仁闻周瑜卧病在床，亲自督帅士兵上阵攻击吴兵。周瑜奋身而起，巡视各营，激励将士杀敌。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">经过一年的交战，周瑜对曹仁杀伤甚众，使得曹仁只好弃城而走。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="27-28" data-ctrmap=":27,:28,">
[27-28]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[27-28]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">孙权任命周瑜为偏将军，兼仁南郡<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%A4%AA%E5%AE%88">太守</a>，并把下隽、汉昌、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%B7%9E%E9%99%B5">州陵</a>三个县作为他的<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%A5%89%E9%82%91">奉邑</a>，让他屯兵于<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%B1%9F%E9%99%B5/4726" data-lemmaid="4726">江陵</a>。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="29" data-ctrmap=":29,">
[29]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[29]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="1_7" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_1_7" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="病卒巴丘" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="1-7" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>病卒巴丘</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%B5%A4%E5%A3%81%E4%B9%8B%E6%88%98/81515" data-lemmaid="81515">赤壁之战</a>后，周瑜向孙权献计软禁刘备，直接管理刘备阵营的军队部属，孙权认为曹操在北方仍需牵制，又认为刘备恐怕难以控制，所以没有采纳。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">建安十五年（210年），孙权批准了周瑜提出征伐益州的方案，周瑜返回驻地江陵，行至巴丘（今湖南岳阳），突然病卒，年仅三十六岁<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="30" data-ctrmap=":30,">
[30]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[30]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
。孙权听闻哭泣道：“公瑾有王佐之资，然而寿命短促，我还能依赖什么呢？”又亲自穿上丧服为周瑜举哀，感动左右。周瑜的灵柩运回吴郡时，孙权到芜湖亲迎，各项丧葬费用，全由国家承担。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="7" data-ctrmap=":7,">
[7]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[7]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
孙权称帝后，对公卿说：“如果没有公瑾，我是当不上皇帝的。”</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="2" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_2" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="主要成就" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-2" label-module="para-title">
<h2 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>主要成就</h2>
<a class="edit-icon j-edit-link" data-edit-dl="2" href="javascript:;"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_edit-lemma"></em>编辑</a>
</div>
<div class="anchor-list">
<a name="2_1" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_2_1" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="开拓江左" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="2-1" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>开拓江左</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">汉献帝兴平二年（195年），周瑜收到了<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E7%AD%96/17360" data-lemmaid="17360">孙策</a>从历阳（今安徽和县）<div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:150px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" nslog-type="9317"
			href="/pic/%E5%91%A8%E7%91%9C/17342/0/42a98226cffc1e17e98a28d94790f603738de925?fr=lemma&ct=single" target="_blank"
		title="周瑜" style="width:150px;height:220px;">
<img  class="lazy-img" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" data-src="https://gss3.bdstatic.com/-Po3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=b737164ca9c27d1ea1263cc62bd4adaf/42a98226cffc1e17e98a28d94790f603738de925.jpg"  alt="周瑜" style="width:150px;height:220px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
周瑜
</span>
</div>送来的书信，来信邀他共下江东。正在寻找政治出路的周瑜收到书信后，马上率领自己的部曲家兵数千人奔赴<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%8E%86%E9%98%B3">历阳</a>。同时，他还带去了大批舟船粮秣。周瑜及江东名士<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%A8%8B%E6%99%AE/69841" data-lemmaid="69841">程普</a>、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%BC%A0%E6%98%AD/4330" data-lemmaid="4330">张昭</a>等人协助孙策先后打下<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%A7%A3%E9%99%B5/85051" data-lemmaid="85051">秣陵</a>、湖孰、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%B1%9F%E4%B9%98">江乘</a>等地，赶走扬州刺史<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%88%98%E7%B9%87">刘繇</a>，占据他的治所<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9B%B2%E9%98%BF">曲阿</a>（今江苏丹阳）。十几天的时间，孙策的军队增加二万余人、战马千匹，威震江东。在继续东进之前，孙策把镇守江东要镇<a target=_blank href="/item/%E4%B8%B9%E9%98%B3/74720" data-lemmaid="74720">丹阳</a>（今江苏南京）的重任委以周瑜。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="31" data-ctrmap=":31,">
[31]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[31]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">后来周瑜拒绝<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%A2%81%E6%9C%AF/16976" data-lemmaid="16976">袁术</a>册封的将军称号，向袁术提出要到<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%B1%85%E5%B7%A2/1258832" data-lemmaid="1258832">居巢</a>（今安徽桐城南）为县长的请求。居巢离长江很近，周瑜的企图是，从居巢顺流而下直奔江东。袁术不知周瑜假途东归的用意，竟满足了周瑜的要求。在居巢，周瑜结识了临淮东城（今安徽定远）的豪族<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%B2%81%E8%82%83/9396" data-lemmaid="9396">鲁肃</a>。在他的劝说之下，鲁肃放弃东城县令的官职，背叛袁术，与周瑜结伴东渡。孙策考虑舒县周氏是<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%BA%90%E6%B1%9F">庐江</a>的名门望族，派周瑜为督，可以充分利用他的家族的社会影响，以招募人马，延揽人才，扩大力量。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="31" data-ctrmap=":31,">
[31]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[31]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">建安四年（199年），孙策与周瑜分率二万余人偷袭<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%9A%96%E5%9F%8E">皖城</a>。轻取皖城后，周瑜随从孙策在寻阳和沙羡，分别打败回师救皖的刘勋以及赶来救援的<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%BB%84%E7%A5%96">黄祖</a>。经过几次大仗，孙策俘获对方部曲士兵三万余人，战船七千余艘，实力大增。通过这次向西用兵，豫章（今江西南昌）、庐陵（今江西吉水西北）一带也尽归江东所有。战争结束后，周瑜以中护军、领江夏太守的职务（孙策授予周瑜这一职务是在取皖城之前）镇守巴丘（今湖南岳阳），防范占据荆州（今湖南、湖北）的刘表东侵。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="31" data-ctrmap=":31,">
[31]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[31]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="2_2" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_2_2" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="联刘抗曹" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="2-2" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>联刘抗曹</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">建安十三年（208年），<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9B%B9%E6%93%8D/6772" data-lemmaid="6772">曹操</a>占领荆州以后，水陆军二十万顺势南下。周瑜向孙权分析了当下形势，如今北方尚未完全平定，<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%A9%AC%E8%B6%85/1201" data-lemmaid="1201">马超</a>、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%9F%A9%E9%81%82/1176067" data-lemmaid="1176067">韩遂</a>还驻兵<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%87%BD%E8%B0%B7%E5%85%B3/447473" data-lemmaid="447473">函谷关</a>以西，是曹操的后患。而正是严寒，曹操的战马也缺乏草料。而且，中原地区的士兵远道跋涉来到江东地区，水土不服，必然会发生疾疫。这几方面是用兵的大患，而曹操都贸然行事。将军抓住曹操的时机，正在今朝。我请求率领精兵数万人，进驻夏口，保证能为将军击破曹操。认为曹操这次来就是来送死的。周瑜的话坚定了孙权抗曹的决心，于是以周瑜为主帅，与刘备联合，火烧赤壁，重创曹操。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="32" data-ctrmap=":32,">
[32]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[32]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="3" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_3" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="人物评价" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-2" label-module="para-title">
<h2 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>人物评价</h2>
<a class="edit-icon j-edit-link" data-edit-dl="3" href="javascript:;"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_edit-lemma"></em>编辑</a>
</div>
<div class="anchor-list">
<a name="3_1" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_3_1" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="后世地位" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="3-1" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>后世地位</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">唐朝建中三年（782年），礼仪使<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%A2%9C%E7%9C%9F%E5%8D%BF/66560" data-lemmaid="66560">颜真卿</a>向唐德宗建议，追封古代名将六十四人，并为他们设庙享奠，当中就包括“吴偏将军南郡太守周瑜”。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="33" data-ctrmap=":33,">
[33]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[33]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
同时代被列入庙享名单的只有关羽、张飞、张辽、吕蒙、陆逊、邓艾、陆抗而已。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">宋朝<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AE%A3%E5%92%8C">宣和</a>五年（1123年），依照唐代惯例，为古代名将设庙，七十二位名将中亦包括周瑜。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="34" data-ctrmap=":34,">
[34]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[34]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
北宋年间成书的《<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%83%E5%8F%B2%E7%99%BE%E5%B0%86%E4%BC%A0">十七史百将传</a>》中，周瑜亦位列其中。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="3_2" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_3_2" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="汉魏" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="3-2" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>汉魏</h3>
</div>
<ul class="custom_dot  para-list list-paddingleft-1"><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E7%AD%96/17360" data-lemmaid="17360">孙策</a>：周公瑾英隽异才，与孤有总角之好，骨肉之分。②吾得卿，谐也。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="7" data-ctrmap=":7,">
[7]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[7]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E6%9D%83/17337" data-lemmaid="17337">孙权</a>：周公瑾雄烈，胆略兼人，遂破孟德，开拓荆州，邈焉难继，君今继之。②（吕蒙）学问开益，筹略奇至，可以次于公瑾，但言议英发不及之耳。③孤非周公瑾，不帝矣。④公瑾有王佐之资，今忽短命，孤何赖哉？⑤孤念公瑾，岂有已乎？⑥此天以君授孤也。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="29" data-ctrmap=":29,">
[29]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[29]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9B%B9%E6%93%8D/6772" data-lemmaid="6772">曹操</a>：赤壁之役，值有疾病，孤烧船自退，横使周瑜虚获此名。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="35" data-ctrmap=":35,">
[35]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[35]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%88%98%E5%A4%87/30564" data-lemmaid="30564">刘备</a>：公瑾文武筹略，万人之英，顾其器量广大，恐不久为人臣耳。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="7" data-ctrmap=":7,">
[7]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[7]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%92%8B%E5%B9%B2/1618736" data-lemmaid="1618736">蒋干</a>：雅量高致，非言辞所间。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="7" data-ctrmap=":7,">
[7]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[7]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%90%95%E8%92%99/6432" data-lemmaid="6432">吕蒙</a>：昔周瑜、程普为左右部督，共攻江陵，虽事决于瑜，普自恃久将，且俱是督，遂共不睦，几败国事。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="36" data-ctrmap=":36,">
[36]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[36]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"></div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%8E%8B%E6%9C%97/6664" data-lemmaid="6664">王朗</a>：周公瑾，江淮之杰，攘臂而为其将。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="37" data-ctrmap=":37,">
[37]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[37]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%A8%8B%E6%99%AE/69841" data-lemmaid="69841">程普</a>：与周公瑾交，若饮醇醪，不觉自醉。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="38" data-ctrmap=":38,">
[38]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[38]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%AF%B8%E8%91%9B%E7%91%BE/18107" data-lemmaid="18107">诸葛瑾</a>、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%AD%A5%E9%AA%98/1767859" data-lemmaid="1767859">步骘</a>：臣窃以瑜昔见宠任，入作心膂，出为爪牙，衔命出征，身当矢石，尽节用命，视死如归，故能摧曹操于乌林，走曹仁于郢都，扬国威德，华夏是震，蠢尔蛮荆，莫不宾服，虽周之方叔，汉之信、布，诚无以尚也。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="29" data-ctrmap=":29,">
[29]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[29]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para">《<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%B1%9F%E8%A1%A8%E4%BC%A0">江表传</a>》：年少有美才<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="29" data-ctrmap=":29,">
[29]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[29]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
。</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%9F%A6%E6%98%AD">韦昭</a>：善谈论，能属文辞，思度弘远，有过人之明。周瑜之后，肃为之冠<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="29" data-ctrmap=":29,">
[29]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[29]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
。</div>
</li></ul><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="3_3" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_3_3" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="两晋" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="3-3" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>两晋</h3>
</div>
<ul class="custom_dot  para-list list-paddingleft-1"><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%99%88%E5%AF%BF/5816" data-lemmaid="5816">陈寿</a>：①曹公乘汉相之资，挟天子而扫群桀，新荡荆城，仗威东夏，于时议者莫不疑贰。周瑜、鲁肃建独断之明，出众人之表，实奇才也。②瑜少精意於音乐<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="29" data-ctrmap=":29,">
[29]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[29]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
。</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%99%86%E6%9C%BA">陆机</a>：①饬法修师，则威德翕赫。宾礼名贤，而张公为之雄；交御豪俊，而周瑜为之杰。彼二君子皆弘敏而多奇，雅达而聪哲，故同方者以类附，等契者以气集，江东盖多士矣。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="39" data-ctrmap=":39,">
[39]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[39]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
②周瑜、陆公、鲁肃、吕蒙之畴入为腹心，出作股肱。</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%A2%81%E5%AE%8F/62475" data-lemmaid="62475">袁宏</a>：①公瑾卓尔，逸志不群。总角料主，则素契于伯符；晚节曜奇，则叁分于赤壁。惜其龄促，志未可量。②公瑾英达，朗心独见。披草求君，定交一面。桓桓魏武，外讬霸迹。志掩衡霍，恃战忘敌。卓卓若人，曜奇赤壁。三光参分，宇宙暂隔。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="40" data-ctrmap=":40,">
[40]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[40]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li></ul><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="3_4" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_3_4" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="唐宋" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="3-4" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>唐宋</h3>
</div>
<ul class="custom_dot  para-list list-paddingleft-1"><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E4%B8%A5%E4%BB%8E">严从</a>：周瑜、鲁肃，咸起诸生，鹗视乌林，鹰扬赤壁。然肃为布衣，当襄汉之际，标卖田宅，分财结士，以求人杰：此其志不小也。公瑾推第於孙策，子敬辍粟於周郎：咸有异於人者也。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="41" data-ctrmap=":41,">
[41]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[41]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9D%8E%E7%99%BD/1043" data-lemmaid="1043">李白</a>：二龙争战决雌雄，赤壁楼船扫地空。烈火初张照云海，周瑜曾此破曹公。</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%83%A1%E6%9B%BE">胡曾</a>：烈火西楚魏帝旗，周郎开国虎争时。交兵不假挥长剑，已破英雄百万师。</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E5%85%83%E6%99%8F">孙元晏</a>：会猎书来举国惊，只应周鲁不教迎。曹公一战奔波后，赤壁功传万古名。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="42" data-ctrmap=":42,">
[42]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[42]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9D%8E%E7%AB%AF/7418704" data-lemmaid="7418704">李端</a>：鸣筝金粟柱，素手玉房前。欲得周郎顾，时时误拂弦。</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9D%8E%E4%B9%9D%E9%BE%84">李九龄</a>：有国由来在得贤，莫言兴废是循环。武侯星落周瑜死，平蜀降吴似等闲。</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%A2%81%E8%82%83/78273" data-lemmaid="78273">梁肃</a>：昔汉纲既解，当涂方炽，利兵南浮，江汉失险。公瑾尝用寡制众，挫强为弱，燎火一举，楼船灰飞。遂乃张吴之臂，壮蜀之趾。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="43" data-ctrmap=":43,">
[43]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[43]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9D%9C%E7%89%A7">杜牧</a>：周有<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%BD%90%E5%A4%AA%E5%85%AC/83747" data-lemmaid="83747">齐太公</a>，秦有<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%8E%8B%E7%BF%A6/37739" data-lemmaid="37739">王翦</a>，两汉有<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%9F%A9%E4%BF%A1/5321" data-lemmaid="5321">韩信</a>、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%B5%B5%E5%85%85%E5%9B%BD">赵充国</a>、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%80%BF%E6%81%AD/20066" data-lemmaid="20066">耿恭</a>、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%99%9E%E8%AF%A9">虞诩</a>、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%AE%B5%E9%A2%8E">段颎</a>，魏有<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%8F%B8%E9%A9%AC%E6%87%BF/9367" data-lemmaid="9367">司马懿</a>，吴有周瑜，蜀有诸葛武侯，晋有<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%BE%8A%E7%A5%9C">羊祜</a>、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9D%9C%E9%A2%84">杜预</a>，梁有<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%9F%A6%E7%9D%BF">韦睿</a>，元魏有<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%B4%94%E6%B5%A9/33894" data-lemmaid="33894">崔浩</a>，周有<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%9F%A6%E5%AD%9D%E5%AE%BD">韦孝宽</a>，隋有<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9D%A8%E7%B4%A0/3688" data-lemmaid="3688">杨素</a>，国朝有<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9D%8E%E9%9D%96/544" data-lemmaid="544">李靖</a>、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9D%8E%E5%8B%A3">李勣</a>、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%A3%B4%E8%A1%8C%E4%BF%AD">裴行俭</a>、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%83%AD%E5%85%83%E6%8C%AF">郭元振</a>。如此人者，当此一时，其所出计画，皆考古校今，奇秘长远，策先定於内，功后成於外。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="44" data-ctrmap=":44,">
[44]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[44]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%8B%8F%E8%BD%BC/53906" data-lemmaid="53906">苏轼</a>：大江东去，浪淘尽。千古风流人物。故垒西边，人道是，三国周郎赤壁。乱石穿空，惊涛拍岸，卷起千堆雪。江山如画，一时多少豪杰！遥想公瑾当年，小乔初嫁了，雄姿英发，<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%BE%BD%E6%89%87%E7%BA%B6%E5%B7%BE">羽扇纶巾</a>， 谈笑间，樯橹灰飞烟灭。故国神游，多情应笑我，早生华发。人生如梦，一樽还酹江月。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="45" data-ctrmap=":45,">
[45]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[45]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%8B%8F%E8%BE%99">苏辙</a>：至于长洲之滨，故城之墟，曹孟德、孙仲谋之所睥睨，周瑜、陆逊之所骋骛，其<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%B5%81%E9%A3%8E%E9%81%97%E8%BF%B9">流风遗迹</a>，亦足以称快世俗。</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%AC%A7%E9%98%B3%E6%BE%88">欧阳澈</a>：使富国强兵，内无动揺，民安如故，有如大夫种之能；转输供馈，外无劳民扰攘之役，有如范蠡之知；临机果断，折冲千里，有如周瑜之勇；度长虑逺，收功于必成，有如赵充国之守。严细柳之军，有如<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E4%BA%9A%E5%A4%AB/6100" data-lemmaid="6100">周亚夫</a>者；奔<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%A1%B9%E7%BE%BD/7005" data-lemmaid="7005">项羽</a>之营，有如<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%A8%8A%E5%93%99">樊哙</a>者；孜孜奉国，知无不为，有如<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%88%BF%E7%8E%84%E9%BE%84">房玄龄</a>者；兼资文武，出将入相，有如<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9D%8E%E9%9D%96/544" data-lemmaid="544">李靖</a>者，则虽愚夫愚妇亦知其可以必胜矣。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="46" data-ctrmap=":46,">
[46]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[46]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%BC%A0%E9%A2%84">张预</a>：孙子曰：“天地孰得？”瑜谓曹公盛寒驱中国士涉江湖。又曰：“亲而离之。”瑜威声远著，而曹公、刘备咸疑谮之是也。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="47" data-ctrmap=":47,">
[47]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[47]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9E%97%E5%85%89%E6%9C%9D">林光朝</a>：当时称之为长才无或异辞者，吴有周瑜、鲁肃、吕蒙、陆逊，蜀有诸葛孔明，是皆一方隽才也。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="48" data-ctrmap=":48,">
[48]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[48]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%99%88%E6%B8%8A/14080201" data-lemmaid="14080201">陈渊</a>：当时人物如周瑜辈，盖百世之士，若其它智勇纷出，莫可悉数。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="49" data-ctrmap=":49,">
[49]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[49]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%99%88%E4%BA%AE/11999960" data-lemmaid="11999960">陈亮</a>：呜呼！使周公瑾而在，其智必及乎此矣。吾观其决谋以破曹操，拓荆州，因欲进取巴蜀，结援<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%A9%AC%E8%B6%85/1201" data-lemmaid="1201">马超</a>以断操之右臂，而还据襄阳以蹙之，此非识大略者不能为也。使斯人不死，当为操之大患，不幸其志未遂而天夺之矣。孙权之称号也，顾群臣曰：周公瑾不在，孤不帝矣。彼亦知吕蒙之徒止足以保据一方，而天下之奇才必也公瑾乎。②昔<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%90%B4%E8%B5%B7/8257" data-lemmaid="8257">吴起</a>与<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%94%B0%E6%96%87/12031" data-lemmaid="12031">田文</a>论功，至主少国疑，大臣未亲，百姓未附之际，吴起屈焉。桓王属大皇于张昭，更以周瑜遗之，后瑜驰驱于颠危之际，昭遂废不用。何哉？江东虽定而国轻矣。余论次其行事，使善观国者有考焉。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="50" data-ctrmap=":50,">
[50]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[50]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%B4%AA%E8%BF%88">洪迈</a>：说者谓天无大风，黄盖不进计，周瑜未必胜。此不善观人者也。方孙权问计于周瑜，瑜已言操冒行四患“将军擒之，宜在今日”；刘备见瑜，恨其兵少，瑜曰：“此自足用，豫州但观瑜破之。”正使无火攻之说，其必有以制服矣。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="51" data-ctrmap=":51,">
[51]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[51]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
孙吴奄有江左，<a target=_blank href="/item/%E4%BA%A2%E8%A1%A1">亢衡</a>中州，固本于策、权之雄略，然一时英杰，如周瑜、鲁肃、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%90%95%E8%92%99/6432" data-lemmaid="6432">吕蒙</a>、陆逊四人者，真所谓社稷心膂，与国为存亡之臣也。</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%8C%83%E6%88%90%E5%A4%A7">范成大</a>：年少曾将<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%A4%BE%E7%A8%B7">社稷</a>扶，三分独数一周瑜。世间豪杰英雄士，江左风流美丈夫。功迹巍巍齐北斗，声名烈烈震东吴。青春年纪归黄壤，提起教人转叹吁。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="52" data-ctrmap=":52,">
[52]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[52]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%B0%A2%E9%87%87%E4%BC%AF">谢采伯</a>：孙策、周瑜拔皖城，纳二乔，皆国色，是以师婚也。英锐豪俊之气，固足办事。毕竟有所溺，则智昏，智昏则防虑疏。策为许贡客箭伤颊，创甚，年二十六卒。瑜为流矢中右协，年三十六卒。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="53" data-ctrmap=":53,">
[53]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[53]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%90%A7%E5%B8%B8">萧常</a>：周瑜从攻横江当利及东渡击枺陵，则知在江北。或曰：此功为大，每以语简而忽之，遂令乌林之役独传。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="54" data-ctrmap=":54,">
[54]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[54]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
瑜、肃建拒操之议，孙权违众用之，卒成大功。然瑜昧于远图，不能乘胜佐昭烈以定中原，乃欲越荆取蜀，而<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%90%95%E8%92%99/6432" data-lemmaid="6432">吕蒙</a>又复袭关羽以取荆州，使曹氏为不讨之贼，可与言知哉？<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="55" data-ctrmap=":55,">
[55]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[55]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%92%B1%E6%97%B6/4265907" data-lemmaid="4265907">钱时</a>：江左之势定于赤壁之一战。曹操破荆州乗胜东下号八十万，向周公瑾决此大计，<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%85%AD%E9%83%A1">六郡</a>之众宁足恃乎？论者遂谓此为公瑾功第一。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="56" data-ctrmap=":56,">
[56]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[56]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li></ul><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="3_5" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_3_5" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="元明清" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="3-5" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>元明清</h3>
</div>
<ul class="custom_dot  para-list list-paddingleft-1"><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%88%98%E7%A5%81">刘祁</a>：已而诸豪割据，士大夫各欲择主立功名，如荀攸、贾诩、程昱、郭嘉、诸葛亮、庞统、鲁肃、周瑜之徒，争以智能自效。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="57" data-ctrmap=":57,">
[57]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[57]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%8E%8B%E4%B9%89%E5%B1%B1/3679963" data-lemmaid="3679963">王义山</a>：某仰惟某官学通六艺，忠贯三精，其谋略则荀攸、贾诩之密，其经济则周瑜、鲁肃之英，其吟啸则谢安、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%BA%BE%E4%BA%AE">庾亮</a>之雅，其牧御则羊祜、陆逊之仁。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="58" data-ctrmap=":58,">
[58]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[58]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%83%A1%E4%B8%89%E7%9C%81">胡三省</a>：此数语所谓相时而动也。然瑜之言不悖大义，鲁肃、吕蒙辈不及也。 <sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="59" data-ctrmap=":59,">
[59]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[59]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E6%89%BF%E6%81%A9/61863" data-lemmaid="61863">孙承恩</a>：矫矫公瑾，实吴良臣，雄姿英发，筹策迈伦，老瞒长驱，志无江表，一战蹙之，功莫与绍。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="60" data-ctrmap=":60,">
[60]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[60]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%99%8F%E7%92%A7">晏璧</a>：当曹操伐吴，威震寰宇，群臣争议迎降，瑜独定大计，度操部水军百万，远渉江湖，不习水土，必生疾病，愿得精兵三万破之，以片言决兴王之策，以偏方抗天下之师，卒走强敌，开拓荆土，非明断能然乎？至其议纵刘备不资其出地，又欲西取巴蜀而并张鲁，北据襄阳以蹙曹操，雄啚出人意表，使究其志，未易量也。虽天啬其寿，中路陨殁，其一举而鼎分三国功名之奇，垂于无穷。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="61" data-ctrmap=":61,">
[61]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[61]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%BC%A0%E5%87%A4%E7%BF%BC/4004312" data-lemmaid="4004312">张凤翼</a>：周公瑾江左伟人，其才略功烈足光纪载，而传必及其顾曲，固知审声知音非尠事也。</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para">黄中坚：周公瑾英姿伟略，诸葛孔明而下一人而已。然其欲徙昭烈于吴，盛宫室美女玩好以娱乐之，分关张各置一处，使如瑜者挟与俱战，则其计亦左矣。昭烈以枭雄之姿，少有大志，其心固欲建霸王之业耳，故髀里肉生至于堕泪。今方破曹操，势可有为，岂甘为吴所豢养？关张与昭烈生死分定，不得昭烈而奉之，岂肯为吴宣力？果若所言，势必将有内变而使魏人得以乘其隙，吴蜀事业俱未可知也。语云：‘知彼知己，百战百胜’。公瑾知昭烈君臣不为人下而顾建此策，殆所谓多思则乱者耶？仲谋于公瑾言无不从而此独不听其见，不岀公瑾上哉！<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="62" data-ctrmap=":62,">
[62]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[62]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%99%88%E5%AD%90%E9%BE%99/53853" data-lemmaid="53853">陈子龙</a>：自汉以后，文武渐分，然犹有<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%99%9E%E8%AF%A9">虞诩</a>、诸葛亮、周瑜、陆逊、司马懿、羊祜、杜预、温峤、谢玄、韦睿、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%B4%94%E6%B5%A9/33894" data-lemmaid="33894">崔浩</a>、李靖、裴行俭、郭元振、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%A3%B4%E5%BA%A6">裴度</a>、李德裕、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%9F%A9%E7%90%A6/16830" data-lemmaid="16830">韩琦</a>、李纲、虞允文之徒奋策儒素建功<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%98%83%E5%A4%96">阃外</a>，为时宗臣。彼岂必有抟虎之力，射雕之技哉？不过深明古今之事，能决机宜之便耳。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="63" data-ctrmap=":63,">
[63]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[63]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%B1%88%E5%A4%A7%E5%9D%87">屈大均</a>：汉唐以来善兵者，率多书生。，若张良、赵充国、邓禹、马援、诸葛孔明、周瑜、鲁肃、杜预、李靖、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%99%9E%E5%85%81%E6%96%87">虞允文</a>之流，莫不沉酣<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%85%AD%E7%BB%8F/32874" data-lemmaid="32874">六经</a>，翩翩文雅，其出奇制胜如风雨之飘忽，如鬼神之变怪。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="64" data-ctrmap=":64,">
[64]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[64]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%BD%97%E8%B4%AF%E4%B8%AD">罗贯中</a>：姿质风流，仪容秀丽。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="65" data-ctrmap=":65,">
[65]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[65]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9D%8E%E8%B4%BD">李贽</a>：周瑜、鲁肃、诸葛瑾、张纮、顾雍，彼比引荐，真君子也。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="66" data-ctrmap=":66,">
[66]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[66]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%83%91%E6%9D%BF%E6%A1%A5/27449" data-lemmaid="27449">郑板桥</a>：周郎年少，正雄姿历落，江东人杰。八十万军飞一炬，风卷滩前黄叶。楼舻云崩，旌旗电扫，射江流血。咸阳三月，火光无此横绝。想他豪竹哀丝，回头顾曲，虎帐谈兵歇。公瑾伯符天挺秀，中道君臣惜别。吴蜀交疏，炎刘鼎沸，老魅成奸黠。至今遗恨，秦淮夜夜幽咽。</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%8E%8B%E6%87%8B%E7%AB%91">王懋竑</a>：周瑜雄略似孙伯符，有并吞中原之志，而不专于自守。</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para">李安溪：规图荆、益，及制曹、刘之策，着着机先，真英物也。②周瑜在则可，如无瑜者，权必不能独挡曹，无玄德则无吴耳，子敬之谋未为非也。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="67" data-ctrmap=":67,">
[67]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[67]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%BC%A0%E4%BD%A9%E7%BA%B6/3387" data-lemmaid="3387">张佩纶</a>：若公瑾则赤壁之后旋没巴邱，世之称公瑾者第曰胆略兼人而已，不知公瑾之才实一世奇才，而驾乎三国群贤之表。吴虽多才，鲁肃失之疏，吕蒙失之谲，陆逊失之柔，孙权以公瑾为王佐，公瑾诚王佐。惜乎！权之非真主才耳。嗟乎！伯符与公瑾实创江东，其意亦欲取荆州袭许都。使天老其才，以与公瑾戮力中原，天下事未可知也。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="68" data-ctrmap=":68,">
[68]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[68]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li></ul><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="3_6" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_3_6" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="近现代" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="3-6" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>近现代</h3>
</div>
<ul class="custom_dot  para-list list-paddingleft-1"><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%8D%A2%E5%BC%BC">卢弼</a>：公瑾生长江、淮，谙识险要，出入彭、蠡，久涉波涛，熟筹彼我，用能以寡击众，遁走阿瞒，一战而霸，克建大勋，玄德谓为本文武筹略，万人之英者，岂虚语哉。或曰：公瑾不死，操之忧也，先主亦安能定蜀乎？<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="69" data-ctrmap=":69,">
[69]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[69]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%94%A1%E4%B8%9C%E8%97%A9">蔡东藩</a>：周瑜年第逾壮，方可有为，乃以意气之未除，遽致短命，不无可惜。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="70" data-ctrmap=":70,">
[70]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[70]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%90%95%E6%80%9D%E5%8B%89">吕思勉</a>：周瑜、鲁肃，亦皆可谓为好乱之士也。徒以二三剽轻之徒，同怀行险徼幸之计，遂肇六十年分裂之祸，岂不哀哉。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="71" data-ctrmap=":71,">
[71]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[71]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%AF%9B%E6%B3%BD%E4%B8%9C/113835" data-lemmaid="113835">毛泽东</a>：周瑜是个“青年团员”，当东吴的统帅，程普等老将不服，后来说服了，还是由了他，结果打了胜仗。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="72" data-ctrmap=":72,">
[72]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[72]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li></ul><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="4" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_4" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="轶事典故" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-2" label-module="para-title">
<h2 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>轶事典故</h2>
<a class="edit-icon j-edit-link" data-edit-dl="4" href="javascript:;"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_edit-lemma"></em>编辑</a>
</div>
<div class="anchor-list">
<a name="4_1" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_4_1" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="顾曲周郎" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="4-1" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>顾曲周郎</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">据《<a target=_blank href="/item/%E4%B8%89%E5%9B%BD%E5%BF%97/1057" data-lemmaid="1057">三国志</a>》记载，周瑜年少时精通音律，即使在喝了三盅酒以后，弹奏者只要有些微的差错，他都能觉察到，并立即会扭头去看那个出错者。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="73" data-ctrmap=":73,">
[73]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[73]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
。自魏晋时代之后，“<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E9%83%8E%E9%A1%BE%E6%9B%B2">周郎顾曲</a>”常作为典故被各大文豪所引用，常常出现于在各类诗歌、戏曲等文学作品中。唐人<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9D%8E%E7%AB%AF/7418704" data-lemmaid="7418704">李端</a>有《<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%90%AC%E7%AD%9D/9269" data-lemmaid="9269">听筝</a>》诗“鸣筝金粟柱，素手玉房前。欲得周郎顾，时时误拂弦。”化用此典故，进一步发挥想象，描绘周郎因相貌英俊，酒酣后更是别有一番风姿。弹奏者多为女子，为了博得他多看一眼，往往故意将曲谱弹错<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="74" data-ctrmap=":74,">
[74]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[74]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="4_2" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_4_2" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="一时瑜亮" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="4-2" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>一时瑜亮</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">罗贯中小说《<a target=_blank href="/item/%E4%B8%89%E5%9B%BD%E6%BC%94%E4%B9%89/5782" data-lemmaid="5782">三国演义</a>》里，作者基于文学艺术需要，周瑜被描写成为与诸葛亮明争暗斗的人物，最终被诸葛亮气死<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="75-76" data-ctrmap=":75,:76,">
[75-76]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[75-76]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
。留下了孔明三气周公瑾，周瑜气的在马上大叫一声，箭疮复裂，坠于马下，临死前仰天长叹：“既生瑜，何生亮！”的故事。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="77-78" data-ctrmap=":77,:78,">
[77-78]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[77-78]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="4_3" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_4_3" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="饮醇自醉" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="4-3" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>饮醇自醉</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">周瑜为人宽宏，唯独程普与他不睦，程普认为自己年长，经常凌辱周瑜。周瑜降低自己身份，始终不与他计较。后来程普敬佩服他，对别人说：”和周公瑾交往，就像喝美酒一样，不知不觉就醉了。“<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="79" data-ctrmap=":79,">
[79]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[79]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
后来用于比喻与宽厚人交，不觉心醉，令人敬服。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="5" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_5" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="亲属成员" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-2" label-module="para-title">
<h2 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>亲属成员</h2>
<a class="edit-icon j-edit-link" data-edit-dl="5" href="javascript:;"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_edit-lemma"></em>编辑</a>
</div>
<div class="anchor-list">
<a name="5_1" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_5_1" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="祖辈" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="5-1" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>祖辈</h3>
</div>
<ul class="custom_dot  para-list list-paddingleft-1"><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para">周景：字仲飨，周瑜<a target=_blank href="/item/%E4%BB%8E%E7%A5%96%E7%88%B6">从祖父</a>（或<a target=_blank href="/item/%E4%BB%8E%E7%A5%96">从祖</a>），周兴之子，官至司空、太尉，追封<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AE%89%E9%98%B3/19696733" data-lemmaid="19696733">安阳</a>乡侯。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="7" data-ctrmap=":7,">
[7]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[7]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
</li></ul><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="5_2" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_5_2" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="父辈" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="5-2" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>父辈</h3>
</div>
<ul class="custom_dot  para-list list-paddingleft-1"><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E5%BC%82/3081661" data-lemmaid="3081661">周异</a>，周瑜之父，洛阳令。</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para">周尚：周瑜从父，周兴之孙（周异之兄，存疑），官至<a target=_blank href="/item/%E4%B8%B9%E6%9D%A8">丹杨</a>太守。</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para">周崇：周瑜从父，周兴之孙，周景长子，嗣安阳乡侯。</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para">周忠：周瑜从父，周景之子，官至太尉、录尚书事。</div>
</li></ul><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="5_3" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_5_3" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="妻妾" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="5-3" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>妻妾</h3>
</div>
<ul class="custom_dot  para-list list-paddingleft-1"><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%B0%8F%E4%B9%94/6488" data-lemmaid="6488">小乔</a>：<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%A1%A5%E5%85%AC">桥公</a>次女，<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%A4%A7%E4%B9%94/17343" data-lemmaid="17343">大乔</a>之妹（古代“桥”与“乔”为一个字。）</div>
</li></ul><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="5_4" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_5_4" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="平辈" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="5-4" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>平辈</h3>
</div>
<ul class="custom_dot  para-list list-paddingleft-1"><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para">周晖：周瑜<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%86%8D%E4%BB%8E%E5%85%84">再从兄</a>，周忠之子，官至洛阳令。</div>
</li></ul><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="5_5" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_5_5" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="子侄" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="5-5" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>子侄</h3>
</div>
<ul class="custom_dot  para-list list-paddingleft-1"><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E5%BE%AA">周循</a>：周瑜长子，官至骑都尉，娶公主<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E9%B2%81%E7%8F%AD">孙鲁班</a>（孙权与<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%AD%A5%E5%A4%AB%E4%BA%BA">步夫人</a>之女）</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E8%83%A4">周胤</a>：周瑜次子，娶孙氏宗室女，兴业都尉，封都乡侯，因罪免</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E5%A6%83">周妃</a>：周瑜之女，一说名为周彻，嫁太子<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AD%99%E7%99%BB">孙登</a>（孙权长子）</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E5%B3%BB">周峻</a>：周瑜兄子，官至偏将军。</div>
</li></ul><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="5_6" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_5_6" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="孙子" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="5-6" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>孙子</h3>
</div>
<ul class="custom_dot  para-list list-paddingleft-1"><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para">周护：周瑜<a target=_blank href="/item/%E4%BB%8E%E5%AD%99">从孙</a>，周峻之子。</div>
</li></ul><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="6" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_6" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="后世纪念" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-2" label-module="para-title">
<h2 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>后世纪念</h2>
<a class="edit-icon j-edit-link" data-edit-dl="6" href="javascript:;"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_edit-lemma"></em>编辑</a>
</div>
<div class="anchor-list">
<a name="6_1" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_6_1" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="墓地" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="6-1" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>墓地</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">周瑜墓中国有多处。据唐朝梁肃所作的《周公瑾墓下诗序》和陆广<a class="lemma-album layout-right nslog:10000206" title="庐江周瑜墓"  href="/pic/%E5%91%A8%E7%91%9C/17342/2640353/b7bc4c667fb21055aa184c32?fr=lemma&ct=cover" target="_blank"  style="width:222px;" nslog-type="10000206">
<div class="album-wrap" style="width:220px;height:165px;">
<img class="picture" alt="庐江周瑜墓" src="https://gss3.bdstatic.com/7Po3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=958d3484e0fe9925cf0c6e5204a95ee4/cc11728b4710b9126758dabfc3fdfc03934522d1.jpg" style="width:220px;height:165px;"/>
</div>
<div class="description">
庐江周瑜墓<span class="number">(13张)</span>
</div>
<div class="albumBg">
<div class="albumBgFir" style="width:214px;"></div>
<div class="albumBgSec" style="width:208px;"></div>
</div>
</a>
微所撰《吴地记》记载<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="80" data-ctrmap=":80,">
[80]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[80]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
，周瑜墓位于苏州，“周瑜坟，在县东二里。 ”</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">据陆游所撰的《南唐书》记载，周瑜墓位于宿州，“瑜葬宿松，即墓为祠，子孙居其旁者，犹数十家。”</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">而据明朝《<a target=_blank href="/item/%E4%B8%80%E7%BB%9F%E5%BF%97">一统志</a>》记载：“周瑜墓在庐江县安丰乡”。公元1422年（明正统七年），提学御史<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%BD%AD%E5%8B%96">彭勖</a>，令知县黄金兰立碑题曰：“吴名将周公瑾之墓”。清《<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%BA%90%E6%B1%9F%E5%8E%BF%E5%BF%97">庐江县志</a>》又载：“周瑜之妻<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%B0%8F%E4%B9%94/6488" data-lemmaid="6488">小乔</a>墓，在西门外真武观西百步，墓墩俗称瑜婆墩”。清<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%92%B8%E4%B8%B0/653" data-lemmaid="653">咸丰</a>年间，墓地被毁。1926年和1942年，周瑜墓先后进行了两次<a target=_blank href="/item/%E4%BF%AE%E7%BC%AE">修缮</a>。<br/>　　1989年春，<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%AE%89%E5%BE%BD%E7%9C%81%E6%96%87%E7%89%A9%E4%BA%8B%E4%B8%9A%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E5%B1%80">安徽省文物事业管理局</a>召开有关专家论证会，对湖南<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%B2%B3%E9%98%B3">岳阳</a>，江西新淦，安徽庐江、巢县、舒城、宿松等地的周瑜墓进行了全面的科学论证，取得一致意见，确认安徽省庐江县的周瑜墓为周瑜<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%A6%96%E4%B8%98">首丘</a>之地。1989年5月，周瑜墓被安徽省人民政府公布为第三批省级重点文物保护单位。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="81" data-ctrmap=":81,">
[81]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[81]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="6_2" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_6_2" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="遗址" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="6-2" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>遗址</h3>
</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para"><div class="lemma-picture text-pic layout-right" style="width:220px; float: right;">
<a class="image-link" nslog-type="9317"
			href="/pic/%E5%91%A8%E7%91%9C/17342/0/cb8065380cd791236c0fcc6caf345982b2b7803f?fr=lemma&ct=single" target="_blank"
		title="周瑜城" style="width:220px;height:165px;">
<img  class="lazy-img" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAMAAAAoyzS7AAAAGXRFWHRTb2Z0d2FyZQBBZG9iZSBJbWFnZVJlYWR5ccllPAAAAAZQTFRF9fX1AAAA0VQI3QAAAAxJREFUeNpiYAAIMAAAAgABT21Z4QAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" data-src="https://gss3.bdstatic.com/-Po3dSag_xI4khGkpoWK1HF6hhy/baike/s%3D220/sign=96f0226222a446237acaa260a8237246/cb8065380cd791236c0fcc6caf345982b2b7803f.jpg"  alt="周瑜城" style="width:220px;height:165px;"/>
</a>
<span class="description">
周瑜城
<sup>[82]</sup>
<a name="ref_[82]_"></a>
</span>
</div>周瑜城位于安徽<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%88%92%E5%9F%8E%E5%8E%BF">舒城县</a>城西南10公里处的干汊河镇瑜城村。为24岁以前的周瑜在家乡修建的兵营，供练兵习武及驻军之用。周瑜城为土城，正方形，长宽各296米，高10米，占地面积104亩，四周是土筑城墙，高城之上是平整的台地，东西南北各有一个相对称的宽六七米的城门。原建有兵营、养马场、周瑜井、拜母堂、净梵寺、古塔等。<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E7%91%9C%E5%9F%8E">周瑜城</a>的西北方向有呈鼎足之势的三个土墩，名曰“练三墩”，传为当年周郎练兵牧马处。周瑜城及练三墩，古称<a target=_blank href="/item/%E7%89%A7%E9%A9%AC%E6%97%A7%E5%B8%82">牧马旧市</a>，为昔日<a target=_blank href="/item/%E9%BE%99%E8%88%92%E5%85%AB%E6%99%AF">龙舒八景</a>之一。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="83" data-ctrmap=":83,">
[83]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[83]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="6_3" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_6_3" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="纪念桥" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="6-3" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>纪念桥</h3>
</div>
<ul class="custom_dot para-list list-paddingleft-1"><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para">周郎桥：周瑜在南京有一处遗迹，即“周郎桥”。据明朝《万历上元县志》载：“周郎桥，在丹阳乡。吴周瑜渡秣陵，破笮融，下湖熟，曾经此，故名。”</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para">周瑜桥：<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%91%A8%E7%91%9C%E6%A1%A5">周瑜桥</a>位于安徽省舒城县带肚堰，位于南门口到码头交叉处，横跨城南护城河；牧马旧市，为周瑜练兵放牧处，“龙舒八景”之一。</div>
</li></ul><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="7" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_7" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="艺术形象" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-2" label-module="para-title">
<h2 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>艺术形象</h2>
<a class="edit-icon j-edit-link" data-edit-dl="7" href="javascript:;"><em class="cmn-icon wiki-lemma-icons wiki-lemma-icons_edit-lemma"></em>编辑</a>
</div>
<div class="anchor-list">
<a name="7_1" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_7_1" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="文学形象" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="7-1" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>文学形象</h3>
</div>
<ul class="custom_dot  para-list list-paddingleft-1"><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><b>小说形象</b></div>
</li></ul><div class="para" label-module="para">小说《<a target=_blank href="/item/%E4%B8%89%E5%9B%BD%E6%BC%94%E4%B9%89/5782" data-lemmaid="5782">三国演义</a>》里为了凸显<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%AF%B8%E8%91%9B%E4%BA%AE/21048" data-lemmaid="21048">诸葛亮</a>的智慧，对历史上的周瑜形象做了较大的改动，并虚构了较多的情节，如赤壁之战，周瑜的主张不太明确，是战是和踌躇不定，诸葛亮借曹操修筑铜雀台欲夺小乔之事，智激周瑜，坚定周瑜抗曹的决心。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="75" data-ctrmap=":75,">
[75]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[75]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
曹操命周瑜同窗好友蒋干劝降周瑜，周瑜设下计策，假装友善，伪造了曹操水军都督<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%94%A1%E7%91%81">蔡瑁</a>、<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%BC%A0%E5%85%81">张允</a>写给周瑜的降书让蒋干发现，上演了一出“<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%92%8B%E5%B9%B2%E7%9B%97%E4%B9%A6/4394846" data-lemmaid="4394846">蒋干盗书</a>”的好戏，为赤壁之战的成功奠定了基础。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">后来周瑜劝诱诸葛亮投吴不成，下定决心必除之而后快。正巧刘备甘夫人去世，周瑜向孙权提出假意要把孙权之妹许配刘备，实则引诱刘备来东吴的妙计。然而在诸葛亮的三个锦囊和吴国太乔国老的“胳膊肘往外拐”的态度下，周瑜的计策被一一化解。诸葛亮三气周瑜，致使周瑜吐血而亡。周瑜死后，孙权厚待他的遗孤。</div>
<div class="para" label-module="para">诸葛亮设计，假装主动为周瑜吊丧，从而给众人留下诸葛亮宽厚大度，周瑜小气不能容人的印象。这是小说里的情节，虽然脍炙人口，但终是虚构事件，与历史不符。<sup class="sup--normal" data-sup="84" data-ctrmap=":84,">
[84]</sup><a class="sup-anchor" name="ref_[84]_6380012">&nbsp;</a>
</div>
<ul class="custom_dot  para-list list-paddingleft-1"><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para"><b>诗词形象</b></div>
</li></ul><div class="para" label-module="para">作为一位青年才俊，周瑜颇受士大夫喜爱称羡，是唐诗宋词里提及频率最高的一位三国人物之一。较为脍炙人口的有，<a target=_blank href="/item/%E6%9D%9C%E7%89%A7">杜牧</a>的“东风不与周郎便，铜雀春深锁二乔”，<a target=_blank href="/item/%E8%8C%83%E6%88%90%E5%A4%A7">范成大</a>的“世间豪杰英雄士，江左风流美丈夫”；。苏轼的《<a target=_blank href="/item/%E5%BF%B5%E5%A5%B4%E5%A8%87%C2%B7%E8%B5%A4%E5%A3%81%E6%80%80%E5%8F%A4">念奴娇·赤壁怀古</a>》“遥想公瑾当年，小乔初嫁了， 雄姿英发。羽扇纶巾， 谈笑间、 强虏灰飞烟灭。”更是描绘出了一代英雄豪杰的洒脱和气度，值得一提的是，“羽扇纶巾”作为常见的儒生打扮，本是苏轼对周瑜的描绘，后来却多化用在诸葛亮身上，成为了诸葛亮的经典形象。</div><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="7_2" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_7_2" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="歇后语" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="7-2" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>歇后语</h3>
</div>
<ul class="custom_dot  para-list list-paddingleft-1"><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para">周瑜打黄盖——一个愿打，一个愿挨</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para">周瑜要饭—— 穷嘟嘟（都督）</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para">周瑜谋荆州——赔了夫人又折兵</div>
</li><li class="list-dot list-dot-paddingleft"><div class="para" label-module="para">诸葛亮哭周瑜——假戏真做</div>
</li></ul><div class="anchor-list">
<a name="7_3" class="lemma-anchor para-title" ></a>
<a name="sub6380012_7_3" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="影视形象" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
<a name="7-3" class="lemma-anchor " ></a>
</div><div class="para-title level-3" label-module="para-title">
<h3 class="title-text"><span class="title-prefix">周瑜</span>影视形象</h3>
</div>

<li class="tashuo-item J-item" data-tashuoId="fb156e672ca44c6144fc2ce2">
<div class="tashuo-author">
<a href="/tashuo/authorcenter?authorId=4a78326fd1e7f74f2e108627" target="_blank">
<div class="ta-author-area"><span><img src="https://imgsa.baidu.com/baike/pic/item/203fb80e7bec54e7179b79fbb0389b504ec26adb.jpg" /></span></div>
<div class="ta-author-slogan-area">
<strong>白马晋一</strong>
<span>代表作《三国其实是个娱乐圈》</span>
</div>
<i></i></a>
</div>
<div class="no-cover">
<p class="title">
<a href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=fb156e672ca44c6144fc2ce2&lemmaId=&fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" target="_blank">
周瑜一生最大对手竟然是他？并非诸葛亮！
</a>
</p>
<p class="abstract">
<a href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=fb156e672ca44c6144fc2ce2&lemmaId=&fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" target="_blank">
刘备的话，孙权也只听了半句。关于周郎英武勃发的评语，孙权自然点头称是，至于功高震主的警言，却是一笑了之，拍着刘备的肩膀，耐人寻味地笑道：妹夫，这酒不醉人人自醉啊，看来，你是喝高了啊。</a>
</p>

</div>
</li>
<li class="tashuo-item J-item" data-tashuoId="9b9d9c1a692c5135d8269e20">
<div class="tashuo-author">
<a href="/tashuo/authorcenter?authorId=5936ecdc32c5dea02c407a20" target="_blank">

<div class="ta-author-slogan-area">
<strong>历史百家争鸣</strong>
<span>历史从未如此丰富多彩</span>
</div>
<i></i></a>
</div>
<a href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=9b9d9c1a692c5135d8269e20&lemmaId=&fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" class="cover" target="_blank">
<img src="https://imgsa.baidu.com/baike/pic/item/5243fbf2b21193138628e9b769380cd791238d49.jpg" data-width="" data-height="" class="cover-img">
<div class="overlay"><img src="https://bkssl.bdimg.com/static/wiki-lemma/widget/lemma_content/mainContent/tashuo/img/overlay_1ccc6d9.png"></div>
<p class="title">
这样的三国人物盘点你看过吗？
</p></a>
<p class="abstract">
<a href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=9b9d9c1a692c5135d8269e20&lemmaId=&fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" target="_blank">
昏庸的主公袁氏家族，四世三公，门徒众多，是东汉末年最具影响力的家族，可惜出了一个庸才——袁绍。导致了袁家的灭亡。官渡之战——袁绍以70万大军逼近曹操7万部队，且袁绍兵多粮足，曹操粮草不足，袁绍下令急行军前进为挫其锐气，田丰谋士箴言，不应急战，应慢战，磨死曹操，袁绍不听，还要...</a>
</p>
<div class="tashuo-operator">
<span class="tashuo-publish-date">2018-03-21</span><span class="tashuo-like J-like " data-isvote="0"><i></i><strong class="J-number">362</strong></span>
</div>
</li>
<li class="tashuo-item J-item" data-tashuoId="465f421a9ea0a8bbf14922fd">
<div class="tashuo-author">
<a href="/tashuo/authorcenter?authorId=4a78326fd1e7f74f2e108627" target="_blank">
<div class="ta-author-area"><span><img src="https://imgsa.baidu.com/baike/pic/item/203fb80e7bec54e7179b79fbb0389b504ec26adb.jpg" /></span></div>
<div class="ta-author-slogan-area">
<strong>白马晋一</strong>
<span>代表作《三国其实是个娱乐圈》</span>
</div>
<i></i></a>
</div>
<div class="no-cover">
<p class="title">
<a href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=465f421a9ea0a8bbf14922fd&lemmaId=&fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" target="_blank">
历史上周瑜小乔究竟什么关系？绝非想象中浪漫！
</a>
</p>
<p class="abstract">
<a href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=465f421a9ea0a8bbf14922fd&lemmaId=&fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" target="_blank">
历史上周瑜小乔的爱情故事真是如此浪漫？我们还是在比较严肃的《三国志》里缕一缕说法吧：“顷之，策欲取荆州，以瑜为中护军，领江夏太守，从攻皖，拔之。时得桥公两女，皆国色也。策自纳大乔，瑜纳小乔。”</a>
</p>
</div>
<div class="tashuo-operator">
<span class="tashuo-publish-date">2017-09-16</span><span class="tashuo-like J-like " data-isvote="0"><i></i><strong class="J-number">335</strong></span>
</div>
</li>
<li class="tashuo-item J-item" data-tashuoId="c88e91fea2ce071a8590db3a">
<div class="tashuo-author">
<a href="/tashuo/authorcenter?authorId=222bebc5db0a5b24b0bd5e21" target="_blank">
<div class="ta-author-area"><span><img src="https://imgsa.baidu.com/baike/pic/item/6609c93d70cf3bc756fb14c4da00baa1cd112a1b.jpg" /></span></div>
<div class="ta-author-slogan-area">
<strong>写乎</strong>
<span>探究历史悬疑，挖掘地方风物</span>
</div>
<i></i></a>
</div>
<a href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=c88e91fea2ce071a8590db3a&lemmaId=&fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" class="cover" target="_blank">
<img src="https://imgsa.baidu.com/baike/pic/item/472309f790529822e237aeaedbca7bcb0a46d453.jpg" data-width="" data-height="" class="cover-img">
<div class="overlay"><img src="https://bkssl.bdimg.com/static/wiki-lemma/widget/lemma_content/mainContent/tashuo/img/overlay_1ccc6d9.png"></div>
<p class="title">
《三国志》里的周瑜与罗贯中笔下的周瑜有什么不同？
</p></a>
<p class="abstract">
<a href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=c88e91fea2ce071a8590db3a&lemmaId=&fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" target="_blank">
周瑜一生东征西战，妻子小乔也陪在他身边。天妒英才，周瑜死时，小乔也不过三十岁左右，乍失佳偶，其悲苦可想而知。她住于庐江，为周郎守墓，抚养遗孤。公元223年，小乔病卒，香消玉殒，享年四十七岁，葬于庐江县城西。</a>
</p>
<div class="tashuo-operator">
<span class="tashuo-publish-date">2018-04-16</span><span class="tashuo-like J-like " data-isvote="0"><i></i><strong class="J-number">264</strong></span>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="slider-item">
<ul class="tashuo-list">
<li class="tashuo-item J-item" data-tashuoId="375a76c42d0177b9f0b9d14c">
<div class="tashuo-author">
<a href="/tashuo/authorcenter?authorId=4a78326fd1e7f74f2e108627" target="_blank">
<div class="ta-author-area"><span><img src="https://imgsa.baidu.com/baike/pic/item/203fb80e7bec54e7179b79fbb0389b504ec26adb.jpg" /></span></div>
<div class="ta-author-slogan-area">
<strong>白马晋一</strong>
<span>代表作《三国其实是个娱乐圈》</span>
</div>
<i></i></a>
</div>
<div class="no-cover">
<p class="title">
<a href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=375a76c42d0177b9f0b9d14c&lemmaId=&fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" target="_blank">
诸葛亮一生中最重要的四个对手是谁？
</a>
</p>
<p class="abstract">
<a href="/tashuo/browse/content?id=375a76c42d0177b9f0b9d14c&lemmaId=&fromLemmaModule=pcBottom" target="_blank">
提起诸葛亮的夙敌，相信绝大多数人首先会想到周瑜。周瑜绝命时“既生瑜，何生亮”的仰天长叹，堪称经典，同时也道明了瑜亮之间的敌对关系。根据《三国演义》描述，周瑜是个心胸狭窄、妒贤忌能的人，想方设法迫害智力高于自己的孔明，结果自己反中了诸葛亮的谋算。</a>
</p>
</div>
<div class="tashuo-operator">
<span class="tashuo-publish-date">2017-03-28</span><span class="tashuo-like J-like " data-isvote="0"><i></i><strong class="J-number">235</strong></span>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
